You will listen to audio files generated by this application and translate individual phrases into a target language either in your mind or aloud. Resulting audio is divided into small paragraphs, each followed by a period of silence which gives you opportunity to summarize the paragraph in target language in your own words either in your mind or aloud. At the beginning, use short paragraphs, not longer than 300 characters because it will help you to remember more text of the original paragraph and thus to formulate your summary more easily.  \r\n\r\nYou can carry the audio files in your mp3 player or smartphone and therefore you can do the exercises on the go, when you are walking, jogging or doing some other menial tasks.  \r\n\r\nWhat is the suitable text?
